1011        <!-- Shortcuts Samples -->
1012
1013
1014        <!-- This section of sample code shows how your application can add shortcuts to -->
1015        <!-- the launcher (home screen).  Shortcuts have a three step life cycle. -->
1016
1017
1018        <!-- 1.  Your application offers to provide shortcuts to the launcher.  When -->
1019        <!-- the user installs a shortcut, an activity within your application -->
1020        <!-- generates the actual shortcut and returns it to the launcher, where it -->
1021        <!-- is shown to the user as an icon. -->
1022
1023
1024        <!-- 2.  Any time the user clicks on an installed shortcut, an intent is sent. -->
1025        <!-- Typically this would then be handled as necessary by an activity within -->
1026        <!-- your application. -->
1027
1028
1029        <!-- 3.  The shortcut is deleted.  There is no notification to your application. -->
1030
1031
1032        <!-- In order provide shortcuts from your application, you provide three things: -->
1033
1034
1035        <!-- 1.  An intent-filter declaring your ability to provide shortcuts -->
1036        <!-- 2.  Code within the activity to provide the shortcuts as requested -->
1037        <!-- 3.  Code elsewhere within your activity, if appropriate, to receive -->
1038        <!-- intents from the shortcut itself. -->
1039
